  • Feature
  • Get Live A B Statistics By Practice

Get statistics batting by practice ok

Request
Method: GET
Route: api/statistics/{practice}/liveab
Example: api/statistics/6239ff31-aa7f-4938-b73b-fb098a19316b/liveab
Route Parameter Pattern Requirement
practice * Required

content-length: 2
content-type: application/json
